## <a name="windows-server-2012-attributes"></a><span data-ttu-id="57675-1914">Windows Server 2012-Attribute</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57675-1914">Windows Server 2012 Attributes</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="57675-1915">Diese Klasse enthält die folgenden Attribute für Windows Server 2012:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="57675-1915">This class contains the following attributes for Windows Server 2012:</span></span>
